</p>

***перси.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перси.html>пе́рси</a> (28110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pьrsь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">пр̏са</i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">pȑsa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">breast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">prs</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">prsia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bosom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перси.html>пе́рси</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pérsi</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перси.html>пе́рсей</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> antiquated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> woman’s breasts, bosom
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  Василий Розанов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vasily_Rozanov" class="extiw" title="w:Vasily Rozanov">Vasily Rozanov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:опавший.html>Опа́вшие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>ли́стья</a></cite>, box 2 and following:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ах.html>Ах́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодеть.html>холоде́ет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодеть.html>холоде́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a>. […] <a href = vnd.unilang:горячность.html>Горя́чность</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сущность.html>су́щность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сущность.html>су́щность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a>.<br />[…] <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пышущий.html>пы́шущие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щеки́</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перси.html>пе́рси</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>ми́ра</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайна.html>та́йны</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лоно.html>ло́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a>.<br /><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ленький</a> Розанов, где́-то <a href = vnd.unilang:закутаться.html>заку́тавшийся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перси.html>пе́рсях</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ax, ne xolodéjet, ne xolodéjet ješčó mir. […] Gorjačnostʹ — súščnostʹ jevó, ljubóvʹ jestʹ súščnostʹ jevó.<br />[…] I pýšuščije ščekí. I <b>pérsi</b> míra. I tájny lóna jevó.<br />I málenʹkij Rozanov, gdé-to zakútavšijsja v jevó <b>pérsjax</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Ah, the world has not yet grown cold. […] Vehemence—the essence of it, love is its essence.<br />[…] And the bursting cheeks. And the <b>bosom</b> of the world. And the secrets of its heart.<br />And little Rozanov, somewhere wrapped up in its <b>bosom</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***персик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:персик.html>пе́рсик</a> (12151)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">përsik</i> (equal to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">pfërsich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pfersich</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:персик.html>пе́рсик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pérsik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:персик.html>пе́рсика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:персик.html>пе́рсики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:персик.html>пе́рсиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>peach (fruit or tree)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перспектива.html>перспекти́ва</a> (3067)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перспектива.html>перспекти́ва</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perspektíva</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перспектива.html>перспекти́вы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перспектива.html>перспекти́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перспектива.html>перспекти́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>perspective <i>(the appearance of depth in objects)</i></li>
<li>vista, prospect</li>
<li>prospect, outlook, look-out, aspects <i>(expected future)</i>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перспектива.html>перспекти́ва</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perspektíva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перспективный.html>перспекти́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perspektívnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)перспекти́внее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)перспекти́вней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перспекти́внейший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>prospective, forward-looking</li>
<li>perspectival</li>
<li>promising</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пьрстьнь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pĭrstĭnĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:перстень.html>пе́рстень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perstenĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pьrsty</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">finger ring; ring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:песенка.html>пе́сенка</a> (4765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pésnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песенка.html>пе́сенка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pésenka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песенка.html>пе́сенки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песенка.html>пе́сенки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песенка.html>пе́сенок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pésnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (little) song
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твоя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:песенка.html>пе́сенка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спетый.html>спе́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tvojá <b>pésenka</b> spéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you're finished; you're history; you're dead</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">your little song is sung</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pěsnь</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песнь.html>песнь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pesnʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сней</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песенный.html>пе́сенный</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песенка.html>пе́сенка</a></b>)
</p>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:песнь.html>Песнь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сней</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Pesnʹ</b> Pésnej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Song of Songs</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a> (1558)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pěsnь</i>, adapted to the common ending <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pésnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>song
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сней</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S <b>pésnej</b> po žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Not a day without a song. (motto)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лебединый.html>лебеди́ная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lebedínaja <b>pésnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">swan song</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лгая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dólgaja <b>pésnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">long story</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:старый.html>ста́рая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stáraja <b>pésnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">same old story</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something very good
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твоя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tvojá nóvaja mašína — prósto <b>pésnja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Your new car really rocks!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">песнетво́рец</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pesnetvórec</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">songwriter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pěsъkъ</i>.

***песочный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:песочный.html>песо́чный</a> (19495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песок.html>песо́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pesók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песочный.html>песо́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pesóčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sand, sandy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песочный.html>песо́чные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pesóčnyje časý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hourglass, sandglass</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sand-coloured</li>
<li><i>(pastry)</i> short
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песочный.html>песо́чное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печенье.html>пече́нье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pesóčnoje pečénʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shortbread, shortcake</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пест</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pest</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестик.html>пе́стик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péstik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестик.html>пе́стика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестик.html>пе́стики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестик.html>пе́стиков</a></b>)

***пестовавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пестовать.html>пе́стовавший</a> (28128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестовать.html>пе́стовавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péstovavšij</span>)
</p>

***пестовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пестовать.html>пе́стовать</a> (28128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pěst-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестовать.html>пе́стовать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péstovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary or stilted</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to nurse, to take care of
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нянчить.html>ня́нчить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">njánčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> stilted</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to educate, to raise
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воспитывать.html>воспи́тывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vospítyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выращивать.html>выра́щивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyráščivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пестреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пестреть.html>пестре́ть</a> (21973)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестрый.html>пёстрый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjóstryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестреть.html>пестре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pestrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to show/appear multicolored
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пестреть.html>пестре́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знамя.html>знамёна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vdalí <b>pestréli</b> znamjóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there was a colourful show of flags in the distance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be multicolored or motley <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive, with/due to something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лица</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пестреть.html>пестре́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:реклама.html>рекла́мой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">úlica <b>pestréjet</b> reklámoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the street is motley due to advertising</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become multicolored or motley</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пестре́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pestrétʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">запестре́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapestrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">запестре́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapestrétʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пестреть.html>пестре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pestrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to look like a kaleidoscope/mosaic <i>(of)</i>, to abound in multicolored things flickering in front of the eyes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:газета.html>газе́ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пестреть.html>пестре́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заголовок.html>заголо́вками</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тема.html>те́му</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gazéty <b>pestréli</b> zagolóvkami na étu tému</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the newspapers carried screaming headlines on the subject</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to abound, to be replete <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, in/with repetitive things</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to be too motley or excessively multicolored</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">запестре́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapestrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***песчаник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:песчаник.html>песча́ник</a> (31948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песчаник.html>песча́ник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pesčánik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песчаник.html>песча́ника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песчаник.html>песча́ники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:песчаник.html>песча́ников</a></b>)
</p>
